       List compares main features of digital single-lens reflex cameras

      <p>
       Following list compares main features of
       <b>
        <a href="/wiki/Digital_single-lens_reflex_camera" title="Digital single-lens reflex camera">
         digital single-lens reflex cameras
        </a>
        (DSLRs)
       </b>
       . Order of this list should be firstly by manufacturer alphabetically, secondly from
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/High_end" title="High end">
        high end
       </a>
       to
       <a href="/wiki/Low-end_market" title="Low-end market">
        low end
       </a>
       models. These are all DSLRs
      </p>

      <p>
       Key:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To save space, the "EOS" is left out from Canon model names.
       </li>
       <li>
        ISO values include maximum sensor range, even if in manual mode ("H1", "Hi 1", etc.)
       </li>
       <li>
        Continuous shooting: fps is "frames per second", indicates the highest speed for full resolution, without separate battery grip (i.e., not integrated into the body).
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Memory_card" title="Memory card">
         Memory card
        </a>
        types: CF is
        <a href="/wiki/CompactFlash" title="CompactFlash">
         CompactFlash
        </a>
        , SD is
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Secure_Digital" title="Secure Digital">
         Secure Digital
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        Dimensions are rounded to the nearest whole number.
       </li>
       <li>
        Weight: with standard battery unless noted otherwise.
       </li>
      </ul>

               </span>

             <a href="/wiki/Articulating_screen" title="Articulating screen">

             </a>

             </sup>

             <a href="/wiki/Touchscreen" title="Touchscreen">
              Touchscreen
             </a>

              T
             </sup>

             <b>
              <a href="/wiki/Nikon_F-mount#AF-P" title="Nikon F-mount">
               AF-P lens
              </a>
             </b>
             support
             <sup>
              −P
             </sup>
             ⋅

             <b>
              AF-P
             </b>
             and without
             <b>
              <a href="/wiki/Nikon_F-mount#E-type_lenses" title="Nikon F-mount">
               E-type lens
              </a>
             </b>
             support
             <sup>
              −E
             </sup>
             ⋅  
Without an
             <b>
              <a href="/wiki/Autofocus" title="Autofocus">
               AF
              </a>
             </b>
             motor (needs
             <b>
              <a href="/wiki/List_of_Nikon_F-mount_lenses_with_integrated_autofocus_motor" title="List of Nikon F-mount lenses with integrated autofocus motor">
               lenses with integrated motor
              </a>
             </b>
             , except
             <a href="/wiki/Nikon_D50" title="Nikon D50">
              D50
             </a>

              *
             </sup>
            </p>
